***koekeloeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koekeloeren.html>koekeloeren</a> (64382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kokeloer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kokerol</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:snail.html>snail</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">coque</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:large.html>large</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hollow.html>hollow</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shell.html>shell</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koekeloeren.html>koekeloeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>To</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:look.html>look</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stare.html>stare</a>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coelde</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koel.html>koel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koelte.html>koelte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koelte.html>koeltes</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koelte.html>koeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coolness, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cold.html>cold</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> freezing <a href = vnd.unilang:temperature.html>temperature</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>possibly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pleasant.html>pleasant</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:breeze.html>breeze</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:any.html>any</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wind.html>wind</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stak.html>stak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:harde.html>harde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:koelte.html>koelte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strong.html>strong</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:breeze.html>breeze</a></b> began <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blow.html>blow</a>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bries.html>bries</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wind.html>wind</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:cool.html>cool</a>, unshakable <a href = vnd.unilang:attitude.html>attitude</a></li></ol>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">caffè</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">قهوه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kahve</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">قَهْوَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qahwa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:coffee.html>coffee</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
